## <a name="introducing-the-net-framework-472"></a><span data-ttu-id="14a5d-120">Představení 4.7.2 rozhraní .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-120">Introducing the .NET Framework 4.7.2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-121">Rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 staví na předchozích verzích rozhraní .NET Framework 4.x přidáním nové opravy mnoha a několik nových funkcí při zbývající velmi stabilní produktu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-121">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 builds on previous versions of the .NET Framework 4.x by adding many new fixes and several new features while remaining a very stable product.</span></span>

### <a name="downloading-and-installing-the-net-framework-472"></a><span data-ttu-id="14a5d-122">Stažení a instalace rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-122">Downloading and installing the .NET Framework 4.7.2</span></span>
 
<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-123">Rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 si můžete stáhnout z těchto míst:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-123">You can download the .NET Framework 4.7.2  from the following locations:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-124">Instalační program webové rozhraní .NET framework 4.7.2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-124">.NET Framework 4.7.2 Web Installer</span></span>](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=863262)

- [<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-125">NET Framework 4.7.2 Offline instalačního programu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-125">NET Framework 4.7.2 Offline Installer</span></span>](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=863265)

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-126">Rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 lze nainstalovat na Windows 10, Windows 8.1, Windows 7 SP1 a odpovídající serverových platforem počínaje systémem Windows Server 2008 R2 SP1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-126">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 can be installed on Windows 10, Windows 8.1, Windows 7 SP1, and the corresponding server platforms starting with Windows Server 2008 R2 SP1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-127">Rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 můžete nainstalovat pomocí instalačního programu webové nebo offline instalačního programu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-127">You can install the .NET Framework 4.7.2 by using either the web installer or the offline installer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-128">Doporučený způsob pro většinu uživatelů je použití webovou Instalační službu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-128">The recommended way for most users is to use the web installer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-129">Rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 v sadě Visual Studio 2012 nebo později po instalaci můžete cílit [rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 Developer Pack](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=874338).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-129">You can target the .NET Framework 4.7.2 in Visual Studio 2012 or later by installing the [.NET Framework 4.7.2 Developer Pack](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=874338).</span></span> 

### <a name="whats-new-in-the-net-framework-472"></a><span data-ttu-id="14a5d-130">Co je nového v rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-130">What's new in the .NET Framework 4.7.2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-131">Rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 obsahuje nové funkce v těchto oblastech:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-131">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 includes new features in the following areas:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-133">ASP.NET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-133">ASP.NET</span></span>](#asp-net472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-134">Síťové služby</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-134">Networking</span></span>](#net472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-135">SQL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-135">SQL</span></span>](#sql472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-136">WPF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-136">WPF</span></span>](#wpf472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-137">ClickOnce</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-137">ClickOnce</span></span>](#ClickOnce472)

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-138">Trvalého fokusu v rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 je vylepšení přístupu, který umožňuje aplikaci poskytnout příslušné prostředí pro uživatele technologie usnadnění.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-138">A continuing focus in the .NET Framework 4.7.2 is improved accessibility, which allows an application to provide an appropriate experience for users of Assistive Technology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-139">Informace o usnadnění zlepšování v rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 najdete v tématu [co je nového v usnadnění v rozhraní .NET Framework](whats-new-in-accessibility.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-139">For information on accessibility improvement in the .NET Framework 4.7.2, see [What's new in accessibility in the .NET Framework](whats-new-in-accessibility.md).</span></span> 

<a name="core-472" />
#### <a name="core"></a><span data-ttu-id="14a5d-140">Jádro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-140">Core</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-141">Rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 funkce velký počet kryptografických vylepšení, lepší podporu dekompresi archivy ZIP a další kolekci rozhraní API.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-141">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 features a large number of cryptographic enhancements, better decompression support for ZIP archives, and additional collection APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-142">**Nové přetížení RSA. Vytvoření a DSA. Vytvoření**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-142">**New overloads of RSA.Create and DSA.Create**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-143"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA.Create(System.Security.Cryptography.DSAParameters)?displayProperty=nameWithType> a <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA.Create(System.Security.Cryptography.RSAParameters)?displayProperty=nameWithType> metody umožňují zadat parametrů klíče, vytvoření nové instance <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA> nebo <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA> klíč.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-143">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA.Create(System.Security.Cryptography.DSAParameters)?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA.Create(System.Security.Cryptography.RSAParameters)?displayProperty=nameWithType> methods let you supply key parameters when instantiated a new <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA> or <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA> key.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-144">Umožňují vám nahraďte kód takto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-144">They allow you to replace code like the following:</span></span>

```csharp
// Before .NET Framework 4.7.2
using (RSA rsa = RSA.Create())
{
   rsa.ImportParameters(rsaParameters);
   // Other code to execute using the RSA instance.
}
``` 

```vb
' Before .NET Framework 4.7.2
Using rsa = RSA.Create()
   rsa.ImportParameters(rsaParameters)
   ' Other code to execute using the rsa instance.
End Using
``` 
<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-145">s kódem takto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-145">with code like this:</span></span>
```csharp
// Starting with .NET Framework 4.7.2
using (RSA rsa = RSA.Create(rsaParameters))
{
   // Other code to execute using the rsa instance.
}
``` 
```vb
' Starting with .NET Framework 4.7.2
Using rsa = RSA.Create(rsaParameters)
   ' Other code to execute using the rsa instance.
End Using
``` 

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-146"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA.Create(System.Int32)?displayProperty=nameWithType> a <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA.Create(System.Int32)?displayProperty=nameWithType> metody umožňují generování nových <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA> nebo <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA> klíče s konkrétní velikost klíče.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-146">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA.Create(System.Int32)?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA.Create(System.Int32)?displayProperty=nameWithType> methods let you generate new <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA> or <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA> keys with a specific key size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-147">Příklad:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-147">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
using (DSA dsa = DSA.Create(2048))
{
   // Other code to execute using the dsa instance.
}
``` 
```vb
Using dsa = DSA.Create(2048)
   ' Other code to execute using the dsa instance.
End Using
``` 

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-148">**Název algoritmu hash přijímal Rfc2898DeriveBytes konstruktory**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-148">**Rfc2898DeriveBytes constructors accept a hash algorithm name**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-149"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Rfc2898DeriveBytes> Třída má tři nové konstruktory s <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.HashAlgorithmName> parametr, který identifikuje algoritmus HMAC s klíčem pro použití při odvozování klíče.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-149">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Rfc2898DeriveBytes> class has three new constructors with a <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.HashAlgorithmName> parameter that identifies the HMAC algorithm to use when deriving keys.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-150">Místo použití SHA-1, vývojáři využít algoritmus SHA-2 a technologií HMAC jako SHA-256, jak je znázorněno v následujícím příkladu:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-150">Instead of using SHA-1, developers should use a SHA-2-based HMAC like SHA-256, as shown in the following example:</span></span>

```csharp
private static byte[] DeriveKey(string password, out int iterations, out byte[] salt, 
                                out HashAlgorithmName algorithm)
{
   iterations = 100000;
   algorithm = HashAlgorithmName.SHA256;

   const int SaltSize = 32;
   const int DerivedValueSize = 32;

   using (Rfc2898DeriveBytes pbkdf2 = new Rfc2898DeriveBytes(password, SaltSize, 
                                                             iterations, algorithm))
   {
      salt = pbkdf2.Salt;
      return pbkdf2.GetBytes(DerivedValueSize);
   }
} 
```
```vb
Private Shared Function DeriveKey(password As String, ByRef iterations As Integer, 
                                  ByRef salt AS Byte(), ByRef algorithm As HashAlgorithmName) As Byte()
   iterations = 100000
   algorithm = HashAlgorithmName.SHA256

   Const SaltSize As Integer = 32
   Const  DerivedValueSize As Integer = 32

   Using pbkdf2 = New Rfc2898DeriveBytes(password, SaltSize, iterations, algorithm)
      salt = pbkdf2.Salt
      Return pbkdf2.GetBytes(DerivedValueSize)
   End Using
End Function 
```

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-151">**Podpora pro dočasné klíče**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-151">**Support for ephemeral keys**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-152">PFX import můžete volitelně načíst privátního klíče přímo z paměti, obcházení pevného disku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-152">PFX import can optionally load private keys directly from memory, bypassing the hard drive.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-153">Pokud nové <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509KeyStorageFlags.EphemeralKeySet?displayProperty=nameWithType> příznak je uveden v <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2> konstruktor nebo jednoho z přetížení <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.Import%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> metoda, privátní klíče budou načteny jako dočasné klíče.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-153">When the new <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509KeyStorageFlags.EphemeralKeySet?displayProperty=nameWithType> flag is specified in an <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2> constructor or one of the overloads of the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.Import%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> method, the private keys will be loaded as ephemeral keys.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-154">To zabrání klíče viditelné na disku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-154">This prevents the keys from being visible on the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-155">Ale:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-155">However:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-156">Vzhledem k tomu, že klíče nejsou uložit trvale na disk, certifikáty načtená nejsou vhodnými kandidáty pro přidání do X509Store tento příznak.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-156">Since the keys are not persisted to disk, certificates loaded with this flag are not good candidates to add to an X509Store.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-157">Klíče načíst tímto způsobem se téměř vždy načítají prostřednictvím CNG systému Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-157">Keys loaded in this manner are almost always loaded via Windows CNG.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-158">Proto musí volající přístup k privátnímu klíči voláním metody rozšíření, jako například [certifikátu. GetRSAPrivateKey()](xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.RSACertificateExtensions.GetRSAPrivateKey%2A).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-158">Therefore, callers must access the private key by calling extension methods, such as [cert.GetRSAPrivateKey()](xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.RSACertificateExtensions.GetRSAPrivateKey%2A).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-159"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.PrivateKey?displayProperty=nameWithType> Vlastnost nebude fungovat.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-159">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.PrivateKey?displayProperty=nameWithType> property does not function.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-160">Od starší verze <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.PrivateKey?displayProperty=nameWithType> vlastnost nefunguje s certifikáty, vývojáři měli provést testů před přepnutím do dočasné klíče.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-160">Since the legacy <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.PrivateKey?displayProperty=nameWithType> property does not work with certificates, developers should perform rigorous testing before switching to ephemeral keys.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-161">**Programové vytvoření PKCS #10 certifikační podpisový požadavků a certifikáty s veřejným klíčem X.509**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-161">**Programmatic creation of PKCS#10 certification signing requests and X.509 public key certificates**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-162">Od verze rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2, může zatížení generovat žádosti o (zástupci oddělení služeb zákazníkům), což umožňuje generování žádost o certifikát do být dvoufázové instalace do existující nástrojů a podepsání certifikátů.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-162">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, workloads can generate certificate signing requests (CSRs), which allows certificate request generation to be staged into existing tooling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-163">To je často užitečné v testovací scénáře.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-163">This is frequently useful in test scenarios.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-164">Další informace a příklady kódu najdete v tématu "programové vytvoření PKCS #10 certifikační podpisový požadavků a certifikáty s veřejným klíčem X.509" v [blogu .NET](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2018/03/08/net-framework-4-7-2-developer-pack-early-access-build-3056-is-available/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-164">For more information and code examples, see "Programmatic creation of PKCS#10 certification signing requests and X.509 public key certificates" in the [.NET Blog](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2018/03/08/net-framework-4-7-2-developer-pack-early-access-build-3056-is-available/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-165">**Nové členy SignerInfo**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-165">**New SignerInfo members**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-166">Od verze rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2, <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo> třída zpřístupňuje další informace o podpis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-166">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo> class exposes more information about the signature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-167">Můžete načíst hodnotu <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo.SignatureAlgorithm?displayProperty=fullName> vlastnost určit algoritmus podpisu používá podepisující osoba.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-167">You can retrieve the value of the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo.SignatureAlgorithm?displayProperty=fullName> property to determine the signature algorithm used by the signer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-168"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo.GetSignature%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> je možné volat získat kopii kryptografický podpis pro tento podepisující osoba.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-168"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo.GetSignature%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> can be called to get a copy of the cryptographic signature for this signer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-169">**Ponechejte zabalené datového proudu otevřené po CryptoStream je zveřejněn.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-169">**Leaving a wrapped stream open after CryptoStream is disposed**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-170">Od verze rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2, <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> třída má další konstruktor, který umožňuje <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream.Dispose%2A> není zavřete zabalené datového proudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-170">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> class has an additional constructor that allows <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream.Dispose%2A> to not close the wrapped stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-171">Chcete nechat otevřený po zabalené datový proud <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> zrušení instance, volejte nové <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> konstruktor následujícím způsobem:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-171">To leave the wrapped stream open after the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> instance is disposed, call the new <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> constructor as follows:</span></span>

```csharp
var cStream = new CryptoStream(stream, transform, mode, leaveOpen: true);
```
```vb
Dim cStream = New CryptoStream(stream, transform, mode, leaveOpen:=true)
```

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-172">**Při dekompresi změny v DeflateStream**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-172">**Decompression changes in DeflateStream**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-173">Od verze rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2, provádění operace dekompresi v <xref:System.IO.Compression.DeflateStream> došlo ke změně třídy používat nativní rozhraní API systému Windows ve výchozím nastavení.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-173">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, the implementation of decompression operations in the <xref:System.IO.Compression.DeflateStream> class has changed to use native Windows APIs by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-174">Obvykle výsledkem zlepšování výkonu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-174">Typically, this results in a substantial performance improvement.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-175">Ve výchozím nastavení pro aplikace, které cílí na rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 je povolena podpora dekompresi pomocí rozhraní API systému Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-175">Support for decompression by using Windows APIs is enabled by default for applications that target .NET Framework 4.7.2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-176">Aplikace, které cílí na starší verze rozhraní .NET Framework, ale jsou spuštěny v rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 se můžete rozhodnout do toto chování přidáním následující [AppContext přepínač](../configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/appcontextswitchoverrides-element.md) do konfiguračního souboru aplikace:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-176">Applications that target earlier versions of .NET Framework but are running under .NET Framework 4.7.2 can opt into this behavior by adding the following [AppContext switch](../configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/appcontextswitchoverrides-element.md) to the application configuration file:</span></span>

```xml
<AppContextSwitchOverrides value="Switch.System.IO.Compression.DoNotUseNativeZipLibraryForDecompression=false" /> 
```

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-177">**Další kolekci rozhraní API**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-177">**Additional collection APIs**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-178">Přidá počet nové rozhraní API pro rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 <xref:System.Collections.Generic.SortedSet%601> a <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> typy.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-178">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 adds a number of new APIs to the <xref:System.Collections.Generic.SortedSet%601> and <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-179">Mezi ně patří:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-179">These include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-180">`TryGetValue` metody, které rozšiřují vzoru zkuste použít v jiné typy kolekcí na tyto dva typy.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-180">`TryGetValue` methods, which extend the try pattern used in other collection types to these two types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-181">Tyto metody jsou:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-181">The methods are:</span></span>
   - [<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-182">' veřejné bool HashSet<T>. TryGetValue (T equalValue, out T actualValue);</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-182">\`public bool HashSet<T>.TryGetValue(T equalValue, out T actualValue);</span></span>](xref:System.Collections.Generic.SortedSet%601.TryGetValue%2A)
   - [<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-183">' veřejné bool SortedSet<T>. TryGetValue (T equalValue, out T actualValue);</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-183">\`public bool SortedSet<T>.TryGetValue(T equalValue, out T actualValue);</span></span>](xref:System.Collections.Generic.SortedSet%601.TryGetValue%2A)
- <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-184">`Enumerable.To*` rozšiřující metody, které převést kolekce <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601>:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-184">`Enumerable.To*` extension methods, which convert a collection to a <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601>:</span></span>
   - [<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-185">Veřejné statické HashSet<TSource> ToHashSet<TSource>(Tato rozhraní IEnumerable<TSource> zdroje);</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-185">public static HashSet<TSource> ToHashSet<TSource>(this IEnumerable<TSource> source);</span></span>](xref:System.Linq.Enumerable.ToHashSet%2A)
   - [<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-186">Veřejné statické HashSet<TSource> ToHashSet<TSource>(Tato rozhraní IEnumerable<TSource> zdroje, IEqualityComparer<TSource> porovnávače);</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-186">public static HashSet<TSource> ToHashSet<TSource>(this IEnumerable<TSource> source, IEqualityComparer<TSource> comparer);</span></span>](xref:System.Linq.Enumerable.ToHashSet%2A)
- <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-187">Nové <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> konstruktory, které vám umožní nastavit kapacity kolekce, která poskytuje výhody výkonu, když víte, velikost <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> předem:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-187">New <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> constructors that let you set the collection's capacity, which yields a performance benefit when you know the size of the <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> in advance:</span></span>
   - <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-188">[veřejné HashSet (int kapacity)](xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601.%23ctor(System.Int32))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-188">[public HashSet(int capacity)](xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601.%23ctor(System.Int32))</span></span>
   - <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-189">[veřejné HashSet (int kapacitu, IEqualityComparer<T> porovnávače)](xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601.%23ctor(System.Int32,System.Collections.Generic.IEqualityComparer%7B%600%7D))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-189">[public HashSet(int capacity, IEqualityComparer<T> comparer)](xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601.%23ctor(System.Int32,System.Collections.Generic.IEqualityComparer%7B%600%7D))</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-190"><xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602> Třída obsahuje nové přetížení <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602.AddOrUpdate%2A> a <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602.GetOrAdd%2A> metody načíst hodnotu ze slovníku nebo ji přidejte, pokud není nalezena a přidejte hodnotu do slovníku nebo jej aktualizovat, pokud již existuje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-190">The <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602> class includes new overloads of the <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602.AddOrUpdate%2A> and <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602.GetOrAdd%2A> methods to retrieve a value from the dictionary or to add it if it is not found, and to add a value to the dictionary or to update it if it already exists.</span></span>

```csharp
public TValue AddOrUpdate<TArg>(TKey key, Func<TKey, TArg, TValue> addValueFactory, Func<TKey, TValue, TArg, TValue> updateValueFactory, TArg factoryArgument)

public TValue GetOrAdd<TArg>(TKey key, Func<TKey, TArg, TValue> valueFactory, TArg factoryArgument)
```

```vb
Public AddOrUpdate(Of TArg)(key As TKey, addValueFactory As Func(Of TKey, TArg, TValue), updateValueFactory As Func(Of TKey, TValue, TArg, TValue), factoryArgument As TArg) As TValue

Public GetOrAdd(Of TArg)(key As TKey, valueFactory As Func(Of TKey, TArg, TValue), factoryArgument As TArg) As TValue
```

<a name="asp-net472" />
#### <a name="aspnet"></a><span data-ttu-id="14a5d-191">ASP.NET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-191">ASP.NET</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-192">**Podpora pro vkládání závislostí v webových formulářů**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-192">**Support for dependency injection in Web Forms**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-193">[Vkládání závislostí (DI)](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/dependency-injection#what-is-dependency-injection) oddělí objekty a jejich závislosti tak, aby kód objektu už je potřeba změnit právě, protože došlo ke změně závislost.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-193">[Dependency injection (DI)](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/dependency-injection#what-is-dependency-injection) decouples objects and their dependencies so that an object's code no longer needs to be changed just because a dependency has changed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-194">Při vývoji aplikace ASP.NET, cílených na rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2, můžete:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-194">When developing ASP.NET applications that target the .NET Framework 4.7.2, you can:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-195">Použít na základě nastavení, založené na rozhraní a na základě konstruktor vkládání v [obslužné rutiny a moduly](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/bb398986.aspx), [stránce instance](xref:System.Web.UI.Page), a [uživatelské ovládací prvky](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/y6wb1a0e.aspx) ASP.NET webové aplikace projekty.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-195">Use setter-based, interface-based, and constructor-based injection in [handlers and modules](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/bb398986.aspx), [Page instances](xref:System.Web.UI.Page), and [user controls](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/y6wb1a0e.aspx) of ASP.NET web application projects.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-196">Použít na základě setter a založený na rozhraní vkládání v [obslužné rutiny a moduly](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/bb398986.aspx), [stránce instance](xref:System.Web.UI.Page), a [uživatelské ovládací prvky](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/y6wb1a0e.aspx) webových projektů ASP.NET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-196">Use setter-based and interface-based injection in [handlers and modules](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/bb398986.aspx), [Page instances](xref:System.Web.UI.Page), and [user controls](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/y6wb1a0e.aspx) of ASP.NET web site projects.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-197">Připojte v různých závislostí vkládání architektury.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-197">Plug in different dependency injection frameworks.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-198">**Podpora pro stejnou lokalitu soubory cookie**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-198">**Support for same-site cookies**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-199">[SameSite](https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-west-first-party-cookies-07) zabrání odesílání souboru cookie spolu s požadavku posílaného mezi weby prohlížeče.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-199">[SameSite](https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-west-first-party-cookies-07) prevents a browser from sending a cookie along with a cross-site request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-200">Přidá rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie.SameSite?displayProperty=nameWithType> vlastnost, jehož hodnota je <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode?displayProperty=nameWithType> – člen výčtu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-200">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 adds a <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie.SameSite?displayProperty=nameWithType> property whose value is a <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode?displayProperty=nameWithType> enumeration member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-201">Pokud je jeho hodnota <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode.Strict?displayProperty=nameWithType> nebo <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode.Lax?displayProperty=nameWithType>, přidá ASP.NET `SameSite` atribut hlavičkou set-cookie.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-201">If its value is <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode.Strict?displayProperty=nameWithType> or <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode.Lax?displayProperty=nameWithType>, ASP.NET adds the `SameSite` attribute to the set-cookie header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-202">SameSite podpora se vztahuje na <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> objekty, stejně jako na <xref:System.Web.Security.FormsAuthentication> a <xref:System.Web.SessionState> soubory cookie.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-202">SameSite support applies to <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> objects, as well as to <xref:System.Web.Security.FormsAuthentication> and <xref:System.Web.SessionState> cookies.</span></span>
 
<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-203">Můžete nastavit SameSite pro <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> objektu následujícím způsobem:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-203">You can set SameSite for an <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> object as follows:</span></span>

```csharp
var c = new HttpCookie("secureCookie", "same origin");
c.SameSite = SameSiteMode.Lax;
```
```vb
Dim c As New HttpCookie("secureCookie", "same origin")
c.SameSite = SameSiteMode.Lax
```
<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-204">Soubory cookie SameSite na úrovni aplikace můžete taky nakonfigurovat úpravou souboru web.config:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-204">You can also configure SameSite cookies at the application level by modifying the web.config file:</span></span>

```xml
<system.web>
   <httpCookies sameSite="Strict" />
</system.web>
```
<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-205">Můžete přidat SameSite pro <xref:System.Web.Security.FormsAuthentication> a <xref:System.Web.SessionState> soubory cookie úpravou souboru webové konfigurace:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-205">You can add SameSite for <xref:System.Web.Security.FormsAuthentication> and <xref:System.Web.SessionState> cookies by modifying the web config file:</span></span>

```xml
<system.web>
   <authentication mode="Forms">
      <forms cookieSameSite="Lax">
         <!-- ...   -->
      </forms>
   <authentication />
   <sessionSate cookieSameSite="Lax"></sessionState>
</system.web>
```

<span data-ttu-id="14a5d-208">Osm vlastnosti, které chcete přidat rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.1 <xref:System.Net.Http.HttpClientHandler?displayProperty=nameWithType> třídy.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-208">The .NET Framework 4.7.1 added eight properties to the <xref:System.Net.Http.HttpClientHandler?displayProperty=nameWithType> class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-209">Však dva došlo <xref:System.PlatformNotSupportedException>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-209">However, two threw a <xref:System.PlatformNotSupportedException>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-210">Rozhraní .NET Framework 4.7.2 teď poskytuje implementaci pro tyto vlastnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-210">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 now provides an implementation for these properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="14a5d-211">Vlastnosti jsou:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="14a5d-211">The properties are:</span></span>
